# Paper Lists of SE Conferences

Research papers accepted by {ICSE, FSE, ASE, ISSTA} since 2020.

### Usage
- Dependency: `scrapy`, `openpyxl`
- Usage: 
    1. add new links in `paper_spider/utils/paperlist.py`
    2. run `scrapy crawl paper_spider`
